function getSunSign(date) {\n            const month = date.getMonth() + 1;\n            const day = date.getDate();\n            \n            for (const [sign, data] of Object.entries(zodiacSigns)) {\n                if ((month === data.dates[0] && day >= data.dates[1]) || \n                    (month === data.dates[2] && day <= data.dates[3])) {\n                    return sign;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            // Default for December 22-31 (Capricorn)\n            return \'Capricorn\';\n        }\n\n        function calculateMoonSign(date, time) {\n            // Simplified moon sign calculation based on date\n            const moonCycle = 29.5; // days\n            const knownNewMoon = new Date(\'2024-01-11\'); // Known new moon date\n            const daysSinceNewMoon = Math.floor((date - knownNewMoon) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));\n            const moonPosition = daysSinceNewMoon % moonCycle;\n            \n            const signs = Object.keys(zodiacSigns);\n            const signIndex = Math.floor((moonPosition / moonCycle) * 12);\n            \n            return signs[signIndex];\n        }\n\n        function calculateRisingSign(date, time, location) {\n            // Simplified rising sign calculation (in real astrology this would need exact time and location)\n            if (!time) {\n                return \'Unknown (requires birth time)\';\n            }\n            \n            const hours = parseInt(time.split(\':\')[0]);\n            const signs = Object.keys(zodiacSigns);\n            const signIndex = Math.floor((hours / 24) * 12);\n            \n            return signs[signIndex];\n        }\n\n        function displayAstrologyResults(sunSign, moonSign, risingSign, birthDate, cleanGoal = goal.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9\\s]/g, \'\').toLowerCase();\n            let numbers = [];\n            \n            for (let char of cleanGoal) {\n                if (/[a-z]/.test(char)) {\n                    numbers.push(char.charCodeAt(0) - 96); // a=1, b=2, etc.\n                } else if (/[0-9]/.test(char)) {\n                    numbers.push(parseInt(char));\n                }\n            }\n            \n            // Create quantum pattern\n            const seed = numbers.reduce((sum, num) => sum + num, 0);\n            const pattern1 = ((seed * 7) % 999) || 111;\n }\n\n        function calculateNumerology(goal) {\n            const cleanGoal = goal.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g, \'\').toLowerCase();\n            let total = 0;\n            \n            for (let char of text) {\n                if (vowels.includes(char)) {\n                    total += char.charCodeAt(0) - 96;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            return total;\n        }\n\n        function calculateConsonants(text) {\n            const vowels = \'aeiou\';\n            let total = 0;\n            \n            for (let char of text) {\n                if (!vowels.includes(char)) {\n                    total += char.charCodeAt(0) - 96;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            return total;\n        }\n\n        function reduceToSingleDigit(number) {\n            while (number > 9) {\n                let sum = 0;\n                while (number > 0) {\n                    sum += number % 10;\n                    number = Math.floor(number / 10);\n                }\n                number = sum;\n            }\n            return number;\n        }\n\n        function interpretCode(code, goal) {\n            const
